|- ( ph -> B e. RR )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.altb


|- ( ph -> A < B )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.f


|- ( ph -> F : ( A (,) B ) --> RR )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.dmdv


|- ( ph -> dom ( RR _D F ) = ( A (,) B ) )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.dvbd


|- ( ph -> E. y e. RR A. x e. ( A (,) B ) ( abs ` ( ( RR _D F ) ` x ) ) <_ y )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.y


|- Y = sup ( ran ( x e. ( A (,) B ) |-> ( abs ` ( ( RR _D F ) ` x ) ) ) , RR , < )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.m


|- M = ( ( |_ ` ( 1 / ( B - A ) ) ) + 1 )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.s


|- S = ( j e. ( ZZ>= ` M ) |-> ( F ` ( B - ( 1 / j ) ) ) )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.r


|- R = ( j e. ( ZZ>= ` M ) |-> ( B - ( 1 / j ) ) )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.n


|- N = if ( M <_ ( ( |_ ` ( Y / ( x / 2 ) ) ) + 1 ) , ( ( |_ ` ( Y / ( x / 2 ) ) ) + 1 ) , M )

Essential: ioodvbdlimc2lem.ch


|- ( ch <-> ( ( ( ( ( ph /\ x e. RR+ ) /\ j e. ( ZZ>= ` N ) ) /\ ( abs ` ( ( S ` j ) - ( limsup ` S ) ) ) < ( x / 2 ) ) /\ z e. ( A (,) B ) ) /\ ( abs ` ( z - B ) ) < ( 1 / j ) ) )

A real function with bounded derivative, has a limit at the upper bound of an open interval. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 11-Dec-2019.) (Proof shortened by AV, 3-Oct-2020.)

Essential: dvnmul.s


|- ( ph -> S e. { RR , CC } )

Essential: dvnmul.x


|- ( ph -> X e. ( ( TopOpen ` CCfld ) |`t S ) )

Essential: dvnmul.a


|- ( ( ph /\ x e. X ) -> A e. CC )

Essential: dvnmul.cc


|- ( ( ph /\ x e. X ) -> B e. CC )

Essential: dvnmul.n


|- ( ph -> N e. NN0 )

Essential: dvnmulf


|- F = ( x e. X |-> A )

Essential: dvnmul.f


|- G = ( x e. X |-> B )

Essential: dvnmul.dvnf


|- ( ( ph /\ k e. ( 0 ... N ) ) -> ( ( S Dn F ) ` k ) : X --> CC )

Essential: dvnmul.dvng


|- ( ( ph /\ k e. ( 0 ... N ) ) -> ( ( S Dn G ) ` k ) : X --> CC )

Essential: dvnmul.c


|- C = ( k e. ( 0 ... N ) |-> ( ( S Dn F ) ` k ) )

Essential: dvnmul.d


|- D = ( k e. ( 0 ... N ) |-> ( ( S Dn G ) ` k ) )

Function-builder for the N -th derivative, product rule. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Theorem: dvnmul


|- ( ph -> ( ( S Dn ( x e. X |-> ( A x. B ) ) ) ` N ) = ( x e. X |-> sum_ k e. ( 0 ... N ) ( ( N _C k ) x. ( ( ( C ` k ) ` x ) x. ( ( D ` ( N - k ) ) ` x ) ) ) ) )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.a


|- ( ( ph /\ i e. I /\ x e. X ) -> A e. CC )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.d


|- ( ph -> D e. Fin )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.e


|- ( ph -> E e. _V )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.db


|- ( ph -> -. E e. D )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.ss


|- ( ph -> ( D u. { E } ) C_ I )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.s


|- ( ph -> S e. { RR , CC } )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.c


|- ( ( ( ph /\ x e. X ) /\ j e. D ) -> C e. CC )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.dvp


|- ( ph -> ( S _D ( x e. X |-> prod_ i e. D A ) ) = ( x e. X |-> sum_ j e. D ( C x. prod_ i e. ( D \ { j } ) A ) ) )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.14


|- ( ( ph /\ x e. X ) -> G e. CC )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.dvf


|- ( ph -> ( S _D ( x e. X |-> F ) ) = ( x e. X |-> G ) )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.f


|- ( i = E -> A = F )

Essential: dvmptfprodlem.cg


|- ( j = E -> C = G )

Induction step for ~ dvmptfprod . (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Theorem: dvmptfprodlem


|- ( ph -> ( S _D ( x e. X |-> prod_ i e. ( D u. { E } ) A ) ) = ( x e. X |-> sum_ j e. ( D u. { E } ) ( C x. prod_ i e. ( ( D u. { E } ) \ { j } ) A ) ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.s


|- ( ph -> S e. { RR , CC } )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.x


|- ( ph -> X e. ( ( TopOpen ` CCfld ) |`t S ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.t


|- ( ph -> T e. Fin )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.h


|- ( ( ph /\ t e. T ) -> ( H ` t ) : X --> CC )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.n


|- ( ph -> N e. NN0 )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.dvnh


|- ( ( ph /\ t e. T /\ j e. ( 0 ... N ) ) -> ( ( S Dn ( H ` t ) ) ` j ) : X --> CC )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.c


|- C = ( s e. ~P T |-> ( n e. NN0 |-> { c e. ( ( 0 ... n ) ^m s ) | sum_ t e. s ( c ` t ) = n } ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.r


|- ( ph -> R C_ T )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.z


|- ( ph -> Z e. ( T \ R ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.ind


|- ( ph -> A. k e. ( 0 ... N ) ( ( S Dn ( x e. X |-> prod_ t e. R ( ( H ` t ) ` x ) ) ) ` k ) = ( x e. X |-> sum_ c e. ( ( C ` R ) ` k ) ( ( ( ! ` k ) / prod_ t e. R ( ! ` ( c ` t ) ) ) x. prod_ t e. R ( ( ( S Dn ( H ` t ) ) ` ( c ` t ) ) ` x ) ) ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.j


|- ( ph -> J e. ( 0 ... N ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem2.d


|- D = ( c e. ( ( C ` ( R u. { Z } ) ) ` J ) |-> <. ( J - ( c ` Z ) ) , ( c |` R ) >. )

Induction step for ~ dvnprodlem2 . (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Theorem: dvnprodlem2


|- ( ph -> ( ( S Dn ( x e. X |-> prod_ t e. ( R u. { Z } ) ( ( H ` t ) ` x ) ) ) ` J ) = ( x e. X |-> sum_ c e. ( ( C ` ( R u. { Z } ) ) ` J ) ( ( ( ! ` J ) / prod_ t e. ( R u. { Z } ) ( ! ` ( c ` t ) ) ) x. prod_ t e. ( R u. { Z } ) ( ( ( S Dn ( H ` t ) ) ` ( c ` t ) ) ` x ) ) ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.s


|- ( ph -> S e. { RR , CC } )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.x


|- ( ph -> X e. ( ( TopOpen ` CCfld ) |`t S ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.t


|- ( ph -> T e. Fin )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.h


|- ( ( ph /\ t e. T ) -> ( H ` t ) : X --> CC )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.n


|- ( ph -> N e. NN0 )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.dvnh


|- ( ( ph /\ t e. T /\ j e. ( 0 ... N ) ) -> ( ( S Dn ( H ` t ) ) ` j ) : X --> CC )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.f


|- F = ( x e. X |-> prod_ t e. T ( ( H ` t ) ` x ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.d


|- D = ( s e. ~P T |-> ( n e. NN0 |-> { c e. ( ( 0 ... n ) ^m s ) | sum_ t e. s ( c ` t ) = n } ) )

Essential: dvnprodlem3.c


|- C = ( n e. NN0 |-> { c e. ( ( 0 ... n ) ^m T ) | sum_ t e. T ( c ` t ) = n } )

The multinomial formula for the k -th derivative of a finite product. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Theorem: dvnprodlem3


|- ( ph -> ( ( S Dn F ) ` N ) = ( x e. X |-> sum_ c e. ( C ` N ) ( ( ( ! ` N ) / prod_ t e. T ( ! ` ( c ` t ) ) ) x. prod_ t e. T ( ( ( S Dn ( H ` t ) ) ` ( c ` t ) ) ` x ) ) ) )

Essential: dvnprod.s


|- ( ph -> S e. { RR , CC } )

Essential: dvnprod.x


|- ( ph -> X e. ( ( TopOpen ` CCfld ) |`t S ) )

Essential: dvnprod.t


|- ( ph -> T e. Fin )

Essential: dvnprod.h


|- ( ( ph /\ t e. T ) -> ( H ` t ) : X --> CC )

Essential: dvnprod.n


|- ( ph -> N e. NN0 )

Essential: dvnprod.dvnh


|- ( ( ph /\ t e. T /\ k e. ( 0 ... N ) ) -> ( ( S Dn ( H ` t ) ) ` k ) : X --> CC )

Essential: dvnprod.f


|- F = ( x e. X |-> prod_ t e. T ( ( H ` t ) ` x ) )

Essential: dvnprod.c


|- C = ( n e. NN0 |-> { c e. ( ( 0 ... n ) ^m T ) | sum_ t e. T ( c ` t ) = n } )

The multinomial formula for the N -th derivative of a finite product. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 5-Apr-2020.)

Theorem: dvnprod


|- ( ph -> ( ( S Dn F ) ` N ) = ( x e. X |-> sum_ c e. ( C ` N ) ( ( ( ! ` N ) / prod_ t e. T ( ! ` ( c ` t ) ) ) x. prod_ t e. T ( ( ( S Dn ( H ` t ) ) ` ( c ` t ) ) ` x ) ) ) )
